You are welcome here exactly as you are. This gathering is a trauma-informed space — there is no pressure to share, perform, or participate in any way that doesn't feel right for your body or your journey. You set the pace.

About the Gathering

Where culture becomes medicine

La Cultura Cura is a culturally rooted, family-centered wellness gathering that honors ancestral healing practices while integrating preventative health education and trauma-informed principles. A bilingual event for the whole family — Body, Mind, and Spirit.

This is not a drop-in fair. It is a guided, structured community experience — woven together by workshops, ceremonial círculos, live music and movement, a shared community meal, and all-day booths and activities.

Now in its third year — built by the community, for the community. Un día dedicado a la curación, la conexión y la comunidad.

💓

Preventative Health

Heart health, diabetes prevention, blood pressure awareness

🌊

Nervous System Care

Breathwork, sound bath, emotional regulation, limbic system education

🌿

Ancestral Wisdom

Cultural pride, tea ceremony, herbs, Indigenous protocols

👨‍👩‍👧

Intergenerational Healing

Family yoga, garden planting, arts & crafts, intergenerational workshops

Concrete Supports

Immigration & legal QR station · Know Your Rights · Health resource tables

2026 Program

A full day of healing

Participants attend two 40-minute workshops across two rounds, choosing from four elemental paths. Facilitator details are being confirmed — check back for updates.

🔥

Fire

Heart Health & Circulation

Medical education integrated with healing touch. Led by Elizabeth, RN.

💧

Water

Emotional Health & Limbic System

Nervous system education and emotional regulation. Led by Tata G.

🌿

Earth

Food, Herbs & Tea Ceremony

Diabetes prevention and tea education. Led by Cura-Te Colectiva.

🌬️

Air

Breath & Family Yoga

Safety, regulation, and releasing fear through breath and movement. Led by Nina.

Full Day Schedule

Registration Opens

Check-in · Photo waiver · Color-coded element name tags · Immigration/legal QR station active · Tlamanalli open

10:00 AM

Desfile Cultural Ceremonial

Ancestral procession led by Tata G · Optional drumming · Youth, families & facilitators process to tlamanalli

10:15 AM

Welcome & Opening Circle

Welcome by Paul · Facilitation by Tata G · Land acknowledgment · Introduction to Four Elements · Blessing of tlamanalli

11:00 AM

Workshop Round 1 40 min

Choose one of four elemental workshops: Fire, Water, Earth, or Air

11:45 AM

Workshop Round 2 40 min

Choose a second, different elemental workshop

1:00 PM

Lunch & Community Hour

Community meal · Tea offered · Vendors active · Garden station continues · Open movement and social connection

Closing Circle Ceremonial

For Communities & Organizations

This model belongs to all of us

La Cultura Cura was built to be replicated. We offer consultation support to help community organizations bring this culturally rooted wellness model to their own people.

01

Operational Blueprint

A tested run-of-show framework adaptable to your community context and scale.

02

Facilitator Curriculum

Workshop structure grounded in trauma-informed practice and the Five Protective Factors.

03

Implementation Support

Direct consultation to help your team plan, staff, and evaluate with cultural integrity.

Request a Consultation →

Register & Connect

There's a place here for you

Whether you're coming to heal, to serve, or to learn — you belong here. Choose the path that feels right for where you are.

🌱

You don't have to share anything you're not ready for. This form helps us prepare a space that truly holds you.

Who will you be attending with?

Would you like our quarterly newsletter?

Your information is kept private and will never be shared without your permission.

🌿 What to Expect

Choose two workshops across two sessions. There are quiet spaces, options for movement, and rest woven throughout the day. Children are welcome and have activities designed just for them.

📋 Surveys & Evaluation

We collect optional pre- and post-event surveys. Your responses help us tell the story of this community's healing and support future gatherings.

📊

Pre-event survey coming soon.
Participation is always optional.

💬 Questions?

You don't have to figure this out alone. Reach out and we'll make sure you feel prepared and held before you arrive.

🤝

Every role matters — from setting up a table to holding space in the closing circle. Tell us how you'd like to show up.

How would you like to contribute?

Would you like our quarterly newsletter?

Your information is kept private and will never be shared without your permission.

📋 Volunteer Roles

We need 20–30 volunteers: registration, campus guides, kitchen staff, tlamanalli guardians, garden leads, floaters, and photographers. Setup begins at 8:00 AM.

🌱 Vendors & Pop-Ups

We welcome 5–8 culturally aligned small businesses — plants, handmade goods, wellness offerings, community art. Vendor sign-up form coming soon.

💛 Every Contribution Matters

This gathering runs on community generosity. Whether you give your time, your hands, your resources, or your presence — you are part of what makes this medicine real.

Would you like our quarterly newsletter?

We respond to all consultation requests within 5–7 business days.

🌱 What We Offer

Consultation to support your team in planning, staffing, facilitating, evaluating, and sustaining a gathering — adapted to your community's specific culture, context, and needs.

📊 Evaluation & Grant Support

We can help you design pre/post surveys, collect community impact data, and use that data to support grant applications and sustainability.

🤝 Rooted in Relationship

We believe in walking alongside communities, not handing down a model. Every consultation starts with deep listening — to your people, your history, and your vision.
